\documentclass[11pt]{article}

    
    
    \usepackage[T1]{fontenc}
    % Nicer default font (+ math font) than Computer Modern for most use cases
    \usepackage{mathpazo}

    % Basic figure setup, for now with no caption control since it's done
    % automatically by Pandoc (which extracts ![](path) syntax from Markdown).
    \usepackage{graphicx}
    % We will generate all images so they have a width \maxwidth. This means
    % that they will get their normal width if they fit onto the page, but
    % are scaled down if they would overflow the margins.
    \makeatletter
    \def\maxwidth{\ifdim\Gin@nat@width>\linewidth\linewidth
    \else\Gin@nat@width\fi}
    \makeatother
    \let\Oldincludegraphics\includegraphics
    % Set max figure width to be 80% of text width, for now hardcoded.
    \renewcommand{\includegraphics}[1]{\Oldincludegraphics[width=.8\maxwidth]{#1}}
    % Ensure that by default, figures have no caption (until we provide a
    % proper Figure object with a Caption API and a way to capture that
    % in the conversion process - todo).
    \usepackage{caption}
    \DeclareCaptionLabelFormat{nolabel}{}
    \captionsetup{labelformat=nolabel}

    \usepackage{adjustbox} % Used to constrain images to a maximum size 
    \usepackage{xcolor} % Allow colors to be defined
    \usepackage{enumerate} % Needed for markdown enumerations to work
    \usepackage{geometry} % Used to adjust the document margins
    \usepackage{amsmath} % Equations
    \usepackage{amssymb} % Equations
    \usepackage{textcomp} % defines textquotesingle
    % Hack from http://tex.stackexchange.com/a/47451/13684:
    \AtBeginDocument{%
        \def\PYZsq{\textquotesingle}% Upright quotes in Pygmentized code
    }
    \usepackage{upquote} % Upright quotes for verbatim code
    \usepackage{eurosym} % defines \euro
    \usepackage[mathletters]{ucs} % Extended unicode (utf-8) support
    \usepackage[utf8x]{inputenc} % Allow utf-8 characters in the tex document
    \usepackage{fancyvrb} % verbatim replacement that allows latex
    \usepackage{grffile} % extends the file name processing of package graphics 
                         % to support a larger range 
    % The hyperref package gives us a pdf with properly built
    % internal navigation ('pdf bookmarks' for the table of contents,
    % internal cross-reference links, web links for URLs, etc.)
    \usepackage{hyperref}
    \usepackage{longtable} % longtable support required by pandoc >1.10
    \usepackage{booktabs}  % table support for pandoc > 1.12.2
    \usepackage[inline]{enumitem} % IRkernel/repr support (it uses the enumerate* environment)
    \usepackage[normalem]{ulem} % ulem is needed to support strikethroughs (\sout)
                                % normalem makes italics be italics, not underlines

\def\PY@reset{\let\PY@it=\relax \let\PY@bf=\relax%
    \let\PY@ul=\relax \let\PY@tc=\relax%
    \let\PY@bc=\relax \let\PY@ff=\relax}
\def\PY@tok#1{\csname PY@tok@#1\endcsname}
\def\PY@toks#1+{\ifx\relax#1\empty\else%
    \PY@tok{#1}\expandafter\PY@toks\fi}
\def\PY@do#1{\PY@bc{\PY@tc{\PY@ul{%
    \PY@it{\PY@bf{\PY@ff{#1}}}}}}}
\def\PY#1#2{\PY@reset\PY@toks#1+\relax+\PY@do{#2}}

    \hypertarget{practicum-differentiaalvergelijkingen-de-lorenz-attractor}{%
\section{Practicum differentiaalvergelijkingen: De Lorenz
Attractor}\label{practicum-differentiaalvergelijkingen-de-lorenz-attractor}}

Link naar notebookviewer:
https://nbviewer.jupyter.org/github/Cubedsheep/practicum-diff-Julia/blob/master/practicum\%20-\%20Julia.ipynb?fbclid=IwAR0w5uD6396VRiiF5jM1AxzXG7EB4HG5WAsDRnNsDRpx\_s\_2yaZP3bjLWWA

Link naar Github: https://github.com/Cubedsheep/practicum-diff-Julia

    

    \hypertarget{importeren-packages}{%
\subsection{Importeren packages}\label{importeren-packages}}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}1}]:} \PY{k}{using} \PY{n}{Plots}
        \PY{k}{using} \PY{n}{Distributed}
        \PY{k}{using} \PY{n}{PyCall}
        \PY{k}{using} \PY{n}{PyPlot}
        \PY{k}{using} \PY{n}{DelimitedFiles}
        \PY{k+kd}{const} \PY{n}{plt} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{PyPlot}
        \PY{n}{ioff}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{using3D}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{c}{\PYZsh{}pygui(true)}
\end{Verbatim}


    Voeg extra `workers' toe om berekeningen parallel te kunnen runnen

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}2}]:} \PY{n}{addprocs}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{9}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{;}
        \PY{n+nd}{@everywhere} \PY{k}{begin}
            \PY{k}{using} \PY{n}{BenchmarkTools}
            \PY{k}{using} \PY{n}{LinearAlgebra}
            \PY{k}{using} \PY{n}{SharedArrays}
            \PY{k}{using} \PY{n}{Printf}
        \PY{k}{end}
\end{Verbatim}

    \hypertarget{definieren-functies-en-variabelen}{%
\subsection{definieren functies en
variabelen}\label{definieren-functies-en-variabelen}}

    Gradiënt implementeert de differentiaalvergelijking. Merk op dat alles
binnen een @everywhere enviroment gewraped zit zodat de functies
beschikbaar zijn voor alle workers

    \hypertarget{dynamische-functies-args-meegeven-aan-gradient}{%
\subsubsection{dynamische functies (args meegeven aan
gradient)}\label{dynamische-functies-args-meegeven-aan-gradient}}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}7}]:} \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} definieer functies en variabelen voor alle workers}
        \PY{n+nd}{@everywhere} \PY{k}{begin}
            \PY{k}{function} \PY{n}{gradient}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{t0}\PY{o}{::}\PY{k+kt}{Float64}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{X}\PY{o}{::}\PY{k+kt}{Array}\PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{k+kt}{Float64}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{arg}\PY{o}{::}\PY{k+kt}{Array}\PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{k+kt}{Float64}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{p}{)}
                \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} de functie die de afeleide van de te zoeken functie geeft}
                \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} in het punt (x, y, z)}
                \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{z}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{X}
                \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{sigma}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{r}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{b}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{arg}

         \PY{c+cm}{ }\PY{c+cm}{ }\PY{c+cm}{ }\PY{c+cm}{ }\PY{c+cm}{r}\PY{c+cm}{e}\PY{c+cm}{t}\PY{c+cm}{u}\PY{c+cm}{r}\PY{c+cm}{n}\PY{c+cm}{s}\PY{c+cm}{:}\PY{c+cm}{ }\PY{c+cm}{t}\PY{c+cm}{u}\PY{c+cm}{p}\PY{c+cm}{l}\PY{c+cm}{e}\PY{c+cm}{ }\PY{c+cm}{m}\PY{c+cm}{e}\PY{c+cm}{t}\PY{c+cm}{ }\PY{c+cm}{t}\PY{c+cm}{i}\PY{c+cm}{j}\PY{c+cm}{d}\PY{c+cm}{,}\PY{c+cm}{ }\PY{c+cm}{a}\PY{c+cm}{f}\PY{c+cm}{s}\PY{c+cm}{t}\PY{c+cm}{a}\PY{c+cm}{n}\PY{c+cm}{d}\PY{c+cm}{ }\PY{c+cm}{e}\PY{c+cm}{n}\PY{c+cm}{ }\PY{c+cm}{i}\PY{c+cm}{n}\PY{c+cm}{d}\PY{c+cm}{e}\PY{c+cm}{x}\PY{c+cm}{ }\PY{c+cm}{(}\PY{c+cm}{T}\PY{c+cm}{,}\PY{c+cm}{ }\PY{c+cm}{d}\PY{c+cm}{,}\PY{c+cm}{ }\PY{c+cm}{i}\PY{c+cm}{n}\PY{c+cm}{d}\PY{c+cm}{e}\PY{c+cm}{x}\PY{c+cm}{)}
         \PY{c+cm}{ }\PY{c+cm}{ }\PY{c+cm}{ }\PY{c+cm}{ }\PY{c+cm}{=\PYZsh{}}
             \PY{k}{function} \PY{n}{find\PYZus{}closest}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x0}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{curve}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{guess}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{h}\PY{p}{)}
                 \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} definieer nieuwe arrays om alleen binnen het opgegeven bereik te zoeken}
                 \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{t1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{t2}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{guess}\PY{p}{;}
                 \PY{n}{len} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{t2}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{n}{t1}\PY{o}{+}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{;}
                 
                 \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} \PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}}
                 \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} vind het punt in curve dat het dichtste ligt}
                 \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} definieer array om afstanden in op te slaan}
                 \PY{n}{dists} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{zeros}\PY{p}{(}\PY{k+kt}{Float64}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{len}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{;}
                 \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} bereken de afstanden}
                 \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{i} \PY{k+kp}{in} \PY{n}{t1}\PY{o}{:}\PY{n}{t2}
                     \PY{n}{dists}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{n}{t1}\PY{o}{+}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{norm}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{curve}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{:}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{n}{x0}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{;}
                 \PY{k}{end}
                 \PY{n}{smallest\PYZus{}distance} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{minimum}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{dists}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{;}
                 \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} index van het punt dat het dichts bij de x0 ligt}
                 \PY{n}{index} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{findfirst}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{isequal}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{smallest\PYZus{}distance}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{dists}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{t1} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{;}
                 
                 \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} \PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}}
                 \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} bereken de afstanden tot de 2 lijnstukken die naast dit punt liggen}
                 \PY{n}{d\PYZus{}line1} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{dist\PYZus{}line\PYZus{}point}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{curve}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{:}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{index}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{curve}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{:}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{index}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{x0}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{;}
                 \PY{n}{d\PYZus{}line2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{dist\PYZus{}line\PYZus{}point}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{curve}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{:}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{index}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{curve}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{:}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{index}\PY{o}{+}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{x0}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{;}
                 
                 \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} \PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}}
                 \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} kijk na of de projecties op de lijnen wel degelijk op de lijnstukken liggen}
                 \PY{n}{P1} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{orth\PYZus{}projection}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{curve}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{:}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{index}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{curve}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{:}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{index}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{x0}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{;}
                 \PY{n}{P2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{orth\PYZus{}projection}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{curve}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{:}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{index}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{curve}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{:}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{index}\PY{o}{+}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{x0}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{;}
                 \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} P = curve\PYZus{}punt + v*di, als curve\PYZus{}punt het eerste punt van het lijnstuk is}
                 \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} en 0\PYZlt{}= di \PYZlt{}= 1, dan ligt de projectie op het lijnstuk}
                 \PY{n}{di1} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x0}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{n}{curve}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{index}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{/}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{curve}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{index}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{n}{curve}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{index}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{;}
                 \PY{n}{di2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x0}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{n}{curve}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{index}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{/}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{curve}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{index}\PY{o}{+}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{n}{curve}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{index}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{;}
                 \PY{n}{on\PYZus{}curve1} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{0} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}=} \PY{n}{di1}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{\PYZam{}\PYZam{}} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{di1} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}=} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{;}
                 \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} \PYZhy{}for debugging\PYZhy{} println(\PYZdq{}lijn1: \PYZdl{}(on\PYZus{}curve1), \PYZdl{}(d\PYZus{}line1)\PYZdq{})}
                 \PY{n}{on\PYZus{}curve2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{0} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}=} \PY{n}{di2}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{\PYZam{}\PYZam{}} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{di2} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}=} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{;}
                 \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} \PYZhy{}for debugging\PYZhy{} println(\PYZdq{}lijn1: \PYZdl{}(on\PYZus{}curve2), \PYZdl{}(d\PYZus{}line2)\PYZdq{})}
                 
                 \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} bereken de tijd}
                 \PY{k}{if} \PY{p}{(}\PY{o}{!}\PY{n}{on\PYZus{}curve1}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{\PYZam{}\PYZam{}} \PY{p}{(}\PY{o}{!}\PY{n}{on\PYZus{}curve2}\PY{p}{)}
                     \PY{n}{T} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{index}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{*}\PY{n}{h}\PY{p}{;}
                     \PY{k}{return} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{T}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{smallest\PYZus{}distance}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{index}\PY{p}{)}
                 \PY{k}{else}
                     \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} een van de 2 projecties ligt zeker op het lijnstuk}
                     \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} op het lijnstuk, dus afstand tot lijn kleiner dan of gelijk aan afstand tot eindpunt}
                     \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{on\PYZus{}curve1} \PY{o}{\PYZam{}\PYZam{}} \PY{p}{(}\PY{o}{!}\PY{n}{on\PYZus{}curve2} \PY{o}{||} \PY{n}{d\PYZus{}line1} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{n}{d\PYZus{}line2}\PY{p}{)}
                         \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} projectie ligt op lijn 1 en afstand kleiner dan projectie2, of projectie2}
                         \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} ligt niet op de lijn: return afstand tot lijn1}
                         \PY{n}{T} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{index}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{o}{+}\PY{n}{di1}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*} \PY{n}{h}\PY{p}{;}
                         \PY{k}{return} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{T}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{d\PYZus{}line1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{index}\PY{p}{)}
                     \PY{k}{else}
                         \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} projectie ligt op lijn 2 en afstand is kleiner dan die tot lijn1}
                         \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} of de projectie ligt niet op lijn 1}
                         \PY{n}{T} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{index}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{o}{+}\PY{n}{di2}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*} \PY{n}{h}\PY{p}{;}
                         \PY{k}{return} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{T}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{d\PYZus{}line2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{index}\PY{p}{)}
                     \PY{k}{end}
                 \PY{k}{end}
                 \PY{k}{return}
             \PY{k}{end}

             \PY{k}{function} \PY{n}{x\PYZus{}dist}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x0}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{curve}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{index}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{T}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{h}\PY{p}{)}
                 
                 \PY{n}{point} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{curve}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{:}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{index}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{;}
                 
                 \PY{k}{if} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{T} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{n}{h}\PY{o}{*}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{index}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
                     \PY{n}{point} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{orth\PYZus{}projection}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{curve}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{:}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{index}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{curve}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{:}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{index}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{x0}\PY{p}{)}
                 \PY{k}{elseif} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{T} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}} \PY{n}{h}\PY{o}{*}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{index}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
                     \PY{n}{point} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{orth\PYZus{}projection}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{curve}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{:}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{index}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{curve}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{:}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{index}\PY{o}{+}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{x0}\PY{p}{)}
                 \PY{k}{end}
                 
                 \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{abs}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{point}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{x0}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
             \PY{k}{end}
         \PY{k}{end}
\end{Verbatim}


    \hypertarget{bereken-heel-exact-de-periode-met-runge-kutta}{%
\subsubsection{bereken heel exact de periode met

    Deze periode wordt gebruikt om een eerste gok te doen waar het punt het
dichtst bij de oplossing zich bevindt

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}17}]:} \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} definieer bereik stapgroottes om te testen}
         \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} (arrays compleet overbodig, gewoon copy\PYZhy{}pasta van hieronder 😛 😝)}
         \PY{n}{num} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}
         \PY{n}{iter} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{o}{:}\PY{n}{num}
         \PY{n}{h} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{iter} \PY{o}{.*} \PY{l+m+mf}{1e\PYZhy{}7}
         \PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{ceil}\PY{o}{.}\PY{p}{(}\PY{k+kt}{Int64}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mf}{1.6} \PY{o}{./} \PY{n}{h}\PY{p}{)}
         \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} los de vergelijkingen op}
         \PY{n}{sol} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{pmap}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{RK4\PYZus{}s}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{fill}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{gradient\PYZus{}s}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{num}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{fill}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x0}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{num}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{h}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{n}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{;}
         \PY{n}{guess} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{ceil}\PY{o}{.}\PY{p}{(}\PY{k+kt}{Int64}\PY{p}{,} \PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mf}{1.54}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mf}{1.57}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{./}\PY{n}{h}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{i} \PY{k+kp}{in} \PY{n}{iter}\PY{p}{]}
         \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} zoek de waarde voor t waar de oplossing het dichtst bij x0 komt}
         \PY{n}{closest} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{pmap}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{find\PYZus{}closest}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{fill}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x0}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{num}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{sol}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{guess}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{h}\PY{p}{)}
         \PY{n}{T} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{closest}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}
\end{Verbatim}

\subsubsection{Methode van Euler}\label{methode-van-euler}}

    Definieer functie die niet heel de oplossing onthoudt

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}21}]:} \PY{n+nd}{@everywhere} \PY{k}{begin}
             \PY{k}{function} \PY{n}{euler\PYZus{}l}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{f}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{x0}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{h}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{n}\PY{p}{)}
                 \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{x0}
                 \PY{n}{min\PYZus{}dist} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{100}
                 \PY{n}{dist} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}
                 \PY{n}{index} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}
         
                 \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{i} \PY{k+kp}{in} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{o}{:}\PY{n}{n}
                     \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{h} \PY{o}{.*} \PY{n}{f}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mf}{0.}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
                     \PY{n}{dist} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{abs}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{x0}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
                     \PY{k}{if} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{i} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}} \PY{n}{n}\PY{o}{/}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{\PYZam{}\PYZam{}} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{dist} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{n}{min\PYZus{}dist}\PY{p}{)}
                         \PY{n}{min\PYZus{}dist} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{dist}
                         \PY{n}{index} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{i}
                     \PY{k}{end}
                 \PY{k}{end}
                 \PY{k}{return} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{min\PYZus{}dist}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{index}\PY{p}{)}
             \PY{k}{end}
         \PY{k}{end}

\subsubsection{Exactere benadering met kleinere
stapgrootte}\label{exactere-benadering-met-kleinere-stapgrootte}}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}12}]:} \PY{c}{\PYZsh{} zoek een betere benadering van de beginwaarde door een kleinere h te nemen}
         \PY{n}{h} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mf}{1e\PYZhy{}5}
         \PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{320001}
         \PY{n}{guess\PYZus{}I} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{290000}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{320000}\PY{p}{]}
         \PY{n}{rounds} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{25}

         \PY{n}{results}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{rounds}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{]}

    \hypertarget{oefening-5}{%
\subsection{Oefening 5}\label{oefening-5}}

    Bereken een beginwaarde die in het vlak ligt waarnaar de oplossingen
rond A worden getrokken. De vergelijking van dit vlak kunnen we
schrijven als: \[(\vec{x}-\vec{A}) \cdot \vec{v_1} = 0\] Als we \(z\)
i.f.v. \(x\) en \(y\) schrijven wordt dit:
\[z = \frac{-v_x(x-a_x)-v_y(y-a_y)}{v_z} + a_z\]

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}17}]:} \PY{n}{v} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{eigA}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{vectors}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{:}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}
         \PY{n}{a} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{matrix}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{A}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{dtype}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{float64}\PY{p}{)}
         \PY{n}{z\PYZus{}val}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{n}{v}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{*}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{n}{a}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{n}{v}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{*}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{n}{a}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{/}\PY{n}{v}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{a}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{]}
\end{Verbatim}
